       Surgical Technologist Schools
      </span>
      <span>
       &gt;&gt;

     <h1 class="slh f3">
      Surgical Technologist Schools
     </h1>
     <div>
      <p>
       If you are considering a certificate in surgical technology, there are about 508 on-campus surgical technologist schools for you to choose from. 
	And there are about 84 online surgical technology schools that you might consider.
      </p>
      <p>
       A reported 5,524 students graduated with a certificate in surgical technology in the US in 2010. 
	The three largest surgical technologist schools, in 2010 in the US, by student population, were:
      </p>
      <ul class="schools">
       <li>
        Houston Community College (Houston, TX)
       </li>
       <li>
        Northern Virginia Community College (Annandale, VA)
       </li>
       <li>
        Lone Star College System (Spring, TX)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2 class="t5">
       Surgical Technology Salaries and Career Outlook
      </h2>
      <p>
       Many of those with a certificate in surgical technology choose to become surgical technologists. 
	If you decide to go this route, you will be joining the ranks of an estimated 183,680 surgical technologists in the US, according to the US Bureau of Labor Statistics. 
	In 2010, California state had the largest population of surgical technologists in the US, with over 8,900 surgical technologists. 
	The government projections show that by 2018, there will be close to 230,650 surgical technologists working around the nation. 
	The projected growth in this field is faster than the projected growth for all careers nationwide.
      </p>
      <p>
       As a surgical technologist you can expect to earn an average salary of $38,727 per year. 
	But, a variety of factors such as seniority or your employer can affect the exact amount your make. 
	Based on these factors, you could earn anywhere from less than $28,753 per year to more than $51,708 per year as a surgical technologist.
      </p>
      <h2 class="t5">
       This Page is Useful for Those Seeking the Following:
      </h2>
      <p>
      </p>

      <h1 class="slh f3">
       Surgical Technologist Schools
      </h1>
      <div class="scrollbar">
       <div class="track">
        <div class="thumb">
         <div class="end">
         </div>

      <div class="viewport">
       <div class="overview t2">
        <p>
         If you are considering a certificate in surgical technology, there are about 508 on-campus surgical technologist schools for you to choose from. 
	And there are about 84 online surgical technology schools that you might consider.
        </p>
        <p>
         A reported 5,524 students graduated with a certificate in surgical technology in the US in 2010. 
	The three largest surgical technologist schools, in 2010 in the US, by student population, were:
        </p>

         <li>
          Houston Community College (Houston, TX)
         </li>
         <li>
          Northern Virginia Community College (Annandale, VA)
         </li>
         <li>
          Lone Star College System (Spring, TX)
         </li>
        </ul>
        <h2 class="t5">
         Surgical Technology Salaries and Career Outlook
        </h2>
        <p>
         Many of those with a certificate in surgical technology choose to become surgical technologists. 
	If you decide to go this route, you will be joining the ranks of an estimated 183,680 surgical technologists in the US, according to the US Bureau of Labor Statistics. 
	In 2010, California state had the largest population of surgical technologists in the US, with over 8,900 surgical technologists. 
	The government projections show that by 2018, there will be close to 230,650 surgical technologists working around the nation. 
	The projected growth in this field is faster than the projected growth for all careers nationwide.
        </p>
        <p>
         As a surgical technologist you can expect to earn an average salary of $38,727 per year. 
	But, a variety of factors such as seniority or your employer can affect the exact amount your make. 
	Based on these factors, you could earn anywhere from less than $28,753 per year to more than $51,708 per year as a surgical technologist.
